Mr. President, I take this opportunity to observe the 100th anniversary of Muir Woods National Historic Park in the State of Washington. This unique historical park is located in the city of Tofino in the south central region of Washington State and contains more than 50 historical examples of the history and culture of northern Washington State. Over the course of the next century, the park will be recognized for the contributions that the community and the Federal Government made to provide opportunities for recreation and education in the region.  Over the years, the park has been the home to many important projects and events, including the construction of the National Bell Telephone Company and the California Pacific Railroad. It was designated an official wilderness in 1972, making the park a true wilderness refuge and allowing citizens to enjoy the rich local history, culture, and natural beauty in the wilderness. In
